24 Mar 2017 17:40:10 : The Wild Weebs, general, Wertfuzzy77#0274, ```py
class Index:
    def __init__(self, Play, Scene, Location):
        self.Play = Play
        self.Scene = Scene
        self.Location = Location

    def __str__(self):
        return "Play {}, Scene {}, Position {}".format(self.Play, self.Scene, self.Location)```
